<div id="review_1155035094" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1155035094" />
    <a title="Helene Jeppesen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21992464-helene-jeppesen"><img alt="Helene Jeppesen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528006866p2/21992464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1155035094?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helene Jeppesen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helene Jeppesen" href="/user/show/21992464-helene-jeppesen">Helene Jeppesen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1155035094" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7770942926597610547">Going into this book was stepping out of my comfort zone. This book is sci-fi and fantasy combined into one, and I'm not good at either of those. However, I was intrigued by all the great reviews out there and I finally started reading. <br/>I was planning on taking my time with this book, especially because I had heard that the beginning could be quite confusing. However, here I am now, 1 1/2 day later - I have finished the book and I am left with a hollow feeling inside. <br/>This story took me by surpr</span>
  <span id="freeText7770942926597610547" style="display:none">Going into this book was stepping out of my comfort zone. This book is sci-fi and fantasy combined into one, and I'm not good at either of those. However, I was intrigued by all the great reviews out there and I finally started reading. <br />I was planning on taking my time with this book, especially because I had heard that the beginning could be quite confusing. However, here I am now, 1 1/2 day later - I have finished the book and I am left with a hollow feeling inside. <br />This story took me by surprise, to say the least! I still don't know what exactly it is about this story that made me love it so much, but I think it was the world building. This takes place in the future, and it was interesting to see how Samantha Shannon focuses on clairvoyance and its effects in the future. I didn't buy it at first, but later - when Shannon combines it with the past - I was sold! <br />The main character Paige was amazing; filled with doubt, loneliness and anger but still actionpacked. I think the fact that she was 19 and not your typical young adult made me love her so much more. Walden was amazing as well! He was mysterious and I LOVED his complicated character. <br />This book has a couple of scenes in it that seem clichés in fantasy, but in this book Shannon makes it work! I rarely find myself in a situation where I want to grab the second book immediately and read on, but that's all I can think about right now. Wow - Samantha Shannon made me love sci-fi :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="7770942926597610547" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MzwZhH1Nh8CIJAzJw5ynD+Nfh23jjsJyZ6xY6+YW46yqCCpAe6gdt7wzHTsSVX8Ct+E4ZmuF7k0CBBSMG7iBqg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w4XdoUlrDKR2dQXEAN4INICtlYMM3bKdwl4GhoLpDwRase5lT46W00JiFDbRF9A51BMqiITWnqKn9krhf0dtAg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8348818467925643349">Samantha Shannon studied English Language and Literature at St. Anne’s College, Oxford. <i>The Bone Season</i>, the first in a seven-book series, was a <i>New York Times</i> bestseller and the inaugural Today Book Club selection. <br/><br/>Her next novel, <i>The Priory of the Orange Tree</i>, was published in February 2019 and became a <i>New York Times</i> and <i>Sunday Times</i> bestseller. Her work has been translated into twenty-six lang</span>
  <span id="freeText8348818467925643349" style="display:none">Samantha Shannon studied English Language and Literature at St. Anne’s College, Oxford. <i>The Bone Season</i>, the first in a seven-book series, was a <i>New York Times</i> bestseller and the inaugural Today Book Club selection. <br /><br />Her next novel, <i>The Priory of the Orange Tree</i>, was published in February 2019 and became a <i>New York Times</i> and <i>Sunday Times</i> bestseller. Her work has been translated into twenty-six languages. She lives in London.</span>
